	purge.keyswitch(14, ne(btn_keyswitches_purge14{unknown}){UserDefined, None}){UserDefined, None}
end on

on persistence_changed
	if(pgs_init{unknown} = 0)
		pgs_init{unknown} := 1
		call reset.keycolors{UserDefined, None}
		call update.keyswitch{UserDefined, None}
		call update.cc_dynamics{UserDefined, None}
		call update.cc_expression{UserDefined, None}
		call update.cc_vibrato{UserDefined, None}
		for i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[keyswitch{unknown}, 1] - 1
			if(keyswitch[i{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.INSTRUMENT{unknown}]{unknown} = instrument.LEGATO{unknown})
				legato.load_arrays(keyswitch[i{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.PREFIX{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
			end if
		end for
		for i{unknown} := 0 to NUM_GROUPS{unknown} - 1
			set_engine_par(ENGINE_PAR_MOD_TARGET_INTENSITY{unknown}, 1000000, i{unknown}, find_mod(i{unknown}, "ENV_AHDSR_VOLUME"){Builtin, None}, find_target(i{unknown}, find_mod(i{unknown}, "ENV_AHDSR_VOLUME"){Builtin, None}, "ENV_AHDSR_VOLUME"){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
		end for
	end if
end on

	if(CC_NUM{unknown} = 111)

		sli_vibIntensity{unknown} := real_to_int(scale.range(int_to_real(CC[101]{unknown}){Builtin, None}, 0, 127, 0, 1e+06){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None}
		call update.cc_vibrato{UserDefined, None}
	end if
	if(CC_NUM{unknown} = 64)
		for key[3]{unknown} := 0 to 16 - 1
			if(keyswitch_mapped_notes[key[3]{unknown}, event_note{unknown}]{unknown} = TRUE{unknown})
				if(keyswitches_pressed[key[3]{unknown}]{unknown} = TRUE{unknown})
					select(keyswitch[key[3]{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.INSTRUMENT{unknown}]{unknown})
					case instrument.SUSTAIN{unknown}

							for key[4]{unknown} := keyswitch[key[3]{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.RANGE_LOW{unknown}]{unknown} to keyswitch[key[3]{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.RANGE_HIGH{unknown}]{unknown}
								sustain_release(key[4]{unknown}, keyswitch_event_notes[key[3]{unknown}, key[4]{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch_event_ids[key[3]{unknown}, key[4]{unknown}]{unknown}, release_id{unknown}, keyswitch[key[3]{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.START_GROUP{unknown}]{unknown} + title_groups{unknown}, keyswitch[key[3]{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch[key[3]{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.RR_COUNT{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
							end for
						end if
					case instrument.LEGATO{unknown}
					end select
				end if
			end if
		end for
	end if
end on

on note
	set_key_pressed(EVENT_NOTE{unknown}, TRUE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	ignore_event(EVENT_ID{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	event_note{unknown} := EVENT_NOTE{unknown}
	event_velocity{unknown} := EVENT_VELOCITY{unknown}
	message("Incoming Note: " & EVENT_NOTE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	if((search[keyswitches{unknown}, event_note{unknown}] # - 1) and (keyswitch[search[keyswitches{unknown}, event_note{unknown}], keyswitch_idx.ACTIVATE{unknown}]{unknown} = TRUE{unknown}))
		for key_it{unknown} := 0 to 16 - 1
			if((keyswitch[key_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.ACTIVATE{unknown}]{unknown} = TRUE{unknown}) and (keyswitch[key_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.NOTE{unknown}]{unknown} # 127))
				if(KEY_DOWN[keyswitches[key_it{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} # TRUE{unknown})
					keyswitches_pressed[key_it{unknown}]{unknown} := FALSE{unknown}
				end if
			end if
		end for
		keyswitches_pressed[search[keyswitches{unknown}, event_note{unknown}]]{unknown} := TRUE{unknown}
		call update.keyswitch{UserDefined, None}
	end if
	for key_it{unknown} := 0 to 16 - 1
		if(keyswitch_mapped_notes[key_it{unknown}, event_note{unknown}]{unknown} = TRUE{unknown})
			if(keyswitches_pressed[key_it{unknown}]{unknown} = TRUE{unknown})
				select(keyswitch[key_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.INSTRUMENT{unknown}]{unknown})
				case instrument.ONE_SHOT{unknown}
					message("one-shot"){Builtin, None}
					one_shot(event_note{unknown}, keyswitch_event_notes[key_it{unknown}, event_note{unknown}]{unknown}, event_velocity{unknown}, keyswitch_event_ids[key_it{unknown}, event_note{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch[key_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.START_GROUP{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch[key_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.RR_COUNT{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch_rr_counter[key_it{unknown}, event_note{unknown}]{unknown}, 0){UserDefined, None}
				case instrument.ADHSR{unknown}
					message("adhsr"){Builtin, None}
					one_shot(event_note{unknown}, keyswitch_event_notes[key_it{unknown}, event_note{unknown}]{unknown}, event_velocity{unknown}, keyswitch_event_ids[key_it{unknown}, event_note{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch[key_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.START_GROUP{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch[key_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.RR_COUNT{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch_rr_counter[key_it{unknown}, event_note{unknown}]{unknown}, - 1){UserDefined, None}
				case instrument.SUSTAIN{unknown}
					message("sustain"){Builtin, None}
					sustain(event_note{unknown}, keyswitch_event_notes[key_it{unknown}, event_note{unknown}]{unknown}, event_velocity{unknown}, keyswitch_event_ids[key_it{unknown}, event_note{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch[key_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.START_GROUP{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch[key_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch[key_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.RR_COUNT{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
				case instrument.LEGATO{unknown}
					legato(event_note{unknown}, keyswitch_event_notes[key_it{unknown}, event_note{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch_event_ids[key_it{unknown}, event_note{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch_event_ids[key_it{unknown}, last_note{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch[key_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.START_GROUP{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch[key_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch[key_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.RR_COUNT{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch[key_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.NUM_TRANSITIONS{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch[key_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.SUSTAIN_FX{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch[key_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.TRANSITION{unknown}]{unknown}, rr_counter[event_note{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
				end select
			end if
		end if
	end for
	event_notes[event_note{unknown}]{unknown} := EVENT_NOTE{unknown}
end on

on release
	release_note{unknown} := EVENT_NOTE{int}
	release_velocity{unknown} := EVENT_VELOCITY{int}
	set_key_pressed(EVENT_NOTE{int}, FALSE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	if(search[keyswitches{unknown}, release_note{unknown}] # - 1)
		if((keyswitch[search[keyswitches{unknown}, release_note{unknown}], keyswitch_idx.ACTIVATE{unknown}]{unknown} = TRUE{unknown}) and (keyswitch[search[keyswitches{unknown}, release_note{unknown}], keyswitch_idx.NOTE{unknown}]{unknown} # 127))
			set_key_pressed(release_note{unknown}, TRUE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end if
	for key_rel_it{unknown} := 0 to 16 - 1
		if(keyswitch_mapped_notes[key_rel_it{unknown}, release_note{unknown}]{unknown} = TRUE{unknown})
			if(keyswitches_pressed[key_rel_it{unknown}]{unknown} = TRUE{unknown})
				select(keyswitch[key_rel_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.INSTRUMENT{unknown}]{unknown})
				case instrument.ONE_SHOT{unknown}
					one_shot_release(release_note{unknown}, keyswitch_event_notes[key_rel_it{unknown}, release_note{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch_event_ids[key_rel_it{unknown}, release_note{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
				case instrument.ADHSR{unknown}
					one_shot_release(release_note{unknown}, keyswitch_event_notes[key_rel_it{unknown}, release_note{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch_event_ids[key_rel_it{unknown}, release_note{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
				case instrument.SUSTAIN{unknown}
					if(CC[64]{unknown} = 0)
						sustain_release(release_note{unknown}, keyswitch_event_notes[key_rel_it{unknown}, release_note{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch_event_ids[key_rel_it{unknown}, release_note{unknown}]{unknown}, release_id{unknown}, keyswitch[key_rel_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.START_GROUP{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch[key_rel_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch[key_rel_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.RR_COUNT{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
					end if
				case instrument.LEGATO{unknown}
					note_held{unknown} := KEY_DOWN[event_note{unknown}]{unknown}
					legato_release(release_note{unknown}, keyswitch_event_notes[key_rel_it{unknown}, release_note{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch_event_ids[key_rel_it{unknown}, release_note{unknown}]{unknown}, release_id{unknown}, keyswitch[key_rel_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.START_GROUP{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch[key_rel_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch[key_rel_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.RR_COUNT{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch[key_rel_it{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.NUM_TRANSITIONS{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
				end select
			end if
		end if
	end for
	event_notes[release_note{unknown}]{unknown} := - 1
end on

on ui_control(sli_envRateCurve{unknown})
	for i{unknown} := 0 to search[vibrato_groups{unknown}, - 1] - 1
		set_engine_par(ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[0]{unknown}, sli_envRateCurve{unknown}, vibrato_groups[i{unknown}]{unknown}, find_mod(vibrato_groups[i{unknown}]{unknown}, "ENV_AHDSR"){Builtin, None}, - 1){Builtin, None}
	end for
	tbl_rate.curve{unknown} := sli_envRateCurve{unknown}
	tbl_rate.attack_point{real} := scale.range.log(int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS{unknown}){Builtin, None} * 0.51, 0, int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS{unknown}){Builtin, None}, 1.5, 0.056){UserDefined, None}
	tbl_rate.release_idx{unknown} := real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS{unknown}){Builtin, None} * 0.75){Builtin, None}
	tbl_rate.attack{real} := scale.range(int_to_real(sli_envRateAttack{unknown}){Builtin, None}, 0, 1e+06, 1.5, tbl_rate.attack_point{real}){UserDefined, None}
	tbl_rate.hold{unknown} := scale.range(sli_envRateHold{unknown}, 0, 1000000, 0, real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS{unknown}){Builtin, None} * 0.15){Builtin, None}){UserDefined, None}
	tbl_rate.decay{real} := scale.range(int_to_real(sli_envRateDecay{unknown}){Builtin, None}, 0, 1e+06, 800, 15000){UserDefined, None}
	tbl_rate.sustain{unknown} := scale.range(sli_envRateSustain{unknown}, 0, 1000000, 0, 1000){UserDefined, None}
	tbl_rate.release{real} := scale.range(int_to_real(750000){Builtin, None}, 0, 1e+06, 800, 40000){UserDefined, None}
	for i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[tbl_rate.env_array{unknown}] - 1
		tbl_rate.expCurve[i{unknown}]{unknown} := real_to_int(exp(tbl_rate.attack{real} * int_to_real(i{unknown}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
		tbl_rate.expCurve[i{unknown}]{unknown} := clamp(tbl_rate.expCurve[i{unknown}]{unknown}, 0, 1000){UserDefined, None}
		tbl_rate.decayCurve[i{unknown}]{unknown} := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i{unknown}){Builtin, None} + scale.range(tbl_rate.decay{unknown}, 800, 15000, 0.01, 11){UserDefined, None})) * tbl_rate.decay{real}) - scale.range(tbl_rate.decay{unknown}, 800, 15000, 0, 200){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None}
		tbl_rate.decayCurve[i{unknown}]{unknown} := clamp(tbl_rate.decayCurve[i{unknown}]{unknown}, 0, 1000){UserDefined, None}
		tbl_rate.decayCurve[i{unknown}]{unknown} := scale.range(tbl_rate.decayCurve[i{unknown}]{unknown}, 0, 1000, tbl_rate.sustain{unknown}, 1000){UserDefined, None}
		tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i{unknown}]{unknown} := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i{unknown}){Builtin, None} + scale.range(tbl_rate.release{unknown}, 800, 15000, 0.01, 5){UserDefined, None})) * tbl_rate.release{real}) - scale.range(tbl_rate.release{unknown}, 800, 15000, 0, 300){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None}
		tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i{unknown}]{unknown} := clamp(tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i{unknown}]{unknown}, 0, 1000){UserDefined, None}
	end for
	tbl_rate.attack_idx{unknown} := search[tbl_rate.expCurve{unknown}, 1000]
	for i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[tbl_rate.env_array{unknown}] - 1
		tbl_rate.linCurve[i{unknown}]{unknown} := real_to_int(scale.range(int_to_real(i{unknown}){Builtin, None}, 0, int_to_real(tbl_rate.attack_idx{unknown}){Builtin, None}, 0, int_to_real(1000){Builtin, None}){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None}
		tbl_rate.logCurve[i{unknown}]{unknown} := 1000 - tbl_rate.expCurve[clamp(tbl_rate.attack_idx{unknown} - i{unknown}, 0, tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS{unknown}){UserDefined, None}]{unknown}
	end for
	for i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[tbl_rate.env_array{unknown}] - 1
		if(tbl_rate.curve{unknown} < 500000)
			tbl_rate.env_array[i{unknown}]{unknown} := (int_to_real(tbl_rate.expCurve[i{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None} * scale.range(int_to_real(clamp(tbl_rate.curve{unknown}, 0, 500000){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None}, 0, 500000, 1, 0){UserDefined, None}) + (int_to_real(tbl_rate.linCurve[i{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None} * scale.range(int_to_real(clamp(tbl_rate.curve{unknown}, 0, 500000){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None}, 0, 500000, 0, 1){UserDefined, None})
		else
			tbl_rate.env_array[i{unknown}]{unknown} := (int_to_real(tbl_rate.linCurve[i{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None} * scale.range(int_to_real(clamp(tbl_rate.curve{unknown}, 500000, 1000000){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None}, 500000, 1e+06, 1, 0){UserDefined, None}) + (int_to_real(tbl_rate.logCurve[i{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None} * scale.range(int_to_real(clamp(tbl_rate.curve{unknown}, 500000, 1000000){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None}, 500000, 1e+06, 0, 1){UserDefined, None})
		end if
		if(i{unknown} > (tbl_rate.attack_idx{unknown} + tbl_rate.hold{unknown}))
			tbl_rate.env_array[i{unknown}]{unknown} := int_to_real(tbl_rate.decayCurve[i{unknown} - (tbl_rate.attack_idx{unknown} + tbl_rate.hold{unknown})]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end for
	for i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[tbl_rate.env_array{unknown}] - 1
		tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i{unknown}]{unknown} := scale.range(tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i{unknown}]{unknown}, 0, 1000, 0, real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[tbl_rate.release_idx{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None}){UserDefined, None}
	end for
	for i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[tbl_rate.env_array{unknown}] - 1
		if(i{unknown} > tbl_rate.release_idx{unknown})
			tbl_rate.env_array[i{unknown}]{unknown} := int_to_real(tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i{unknown} - tbl_rate.release_idx{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end for
	for i{unknown} := 0 to tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS{unknown} - 1
		tbl_rate1[i{unknown}]{unknown} := scale.range(clamp(real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None}, 0, 1000){UserDefined, None}, 0, 1000, 0, real_to_int(int_to_real(1000){Builtin, None} * 0.88){Builtin, None}){UserDefined, None}
		tbl_rate2[i{unknown}]{unknown} := tbl_rate1[i{unknown}]{unknown}
	end for
	lbl_envRateCurve{unknown} -> text := get_engine_par_disp(ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[0]{unknown}, vibrato_groups[0]{unknown}, find_mod(vibrato_groups[0]{unknown}, "ENV_AHDSR"){Builtin, None}, - 1){Builtin, None} & " " & ADHSR_UNITS[0]{unknown}
	if(0 = 4)
		lbl_envRateCurve{unknown} -> text := (sli_envRateCurve{unknown} / 10000) & " %"
	end if
	last_time_envRateCurve{unknown} := ENGINE_UPTIME{int}
	wait(800 * 1000){Builtin, None}
	if((ENGINE_UPTIME{int} - last_time_envRateCurve{unknown}) > (800 - 5))
		set_text(lbl_envRateCurve{unknown}, envRateNames[0]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	end if
end on

on ui_control(btn_prevPreset{unknown})
	btn_prevPreset{unknown} := FALSE{unknown}
	mnu_preset{unknown} := ((mnu_preset{unknown} - 1) + presetCount{unknown}) mod presetCount{unknown}
	call update.preset.menu{UserDefined, None}
	if(presetCount{unknown} # 0)
		load.preset{UserDefined, None}
	end if
end on

on ui_control(btn_nextPreset{unknown})
	btn_nextPreset{unknown} := FALSE{unknown}
	mnu_preset{unknown} := (mnu_preset{unknown} + 1) mod presetCount{unknown}
	call update.preset.menu{UserDefined, None}
	if(presetCount{unknown} # 0)
		load.preset{UserDefined, None}
	end if
end on

	btn_savePreset{unknown} := FALSE{unknown}
	save.preset{UserDefined, None}
end on

on ui_control(btn_deletePreset{unknown})
	btn_deletePreset{unknown} := FALSE{unknown}
	delete.preset{UserDefined, None}
end on

on ui_control(mouse_nka{unknown})
	if(NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE{unknown} = NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_DROP{unknown})
		wait_async(load_array_str(vibrato_preset{unknown}, NI_DND_ITEMS_ARRAY[0]{string}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
		call load.array{UserDefined, None}
	end if
end on

on ui_control(btn_scanPresets{unknown})
	if(preset_scan{unknown} = FALSE{unknown})
		preset_scan{unknown} := TRUE{unknown}
		for i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[vibPresetCount{unknown}] - 1
			vibPresetCount[i{unknown}]{unknown} := 0
			vibPresetNames[i{unknown}]{unknown} := ""
		end for
		array.clear(vibrato_preset2{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
		array.clear(vibrato_preset{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
		presetCount{unknown} := 0
		fs_navigate(get_ui_id(file_browser{unknown}){Builtin, None}, 1){Builtin, None}
	end if
end on

on ui_control(file_browser{unknown})
	message("File Browser triggered"){Builtin, None}
	wait_async(load_array_str(vibrato_preset{unknown}, fs_get_filename(get_ui_id(file_browser{unknown}){Builtin, None}, 2){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	if((preset_scan{unknown} = TRUE{unknown}) and (vibrato_preset[preset_idx.DELETED{unknown}]{unknown} # - 420))
		if(vibrato_preset[preset_idx.DELETED{unknown}]{unknown} = 0)
			if(not array_equal(vibrato_preset{unknown}, vibrato_preset2{unknown}){Builtin, None})
				vibPresetNames[presetCount{unknown}]{unknown} := fs_get_filename(get_ui_id(file_browser{unknown}){Builtin, None}, 0){Builtin, None}
				vibPresetCount[presetCount{unknown}]{unknown} := 1
				inc(presetCount{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			end if
			array.clear(vibrato_preset{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
		else
			if(((vibrato_preset[preset_idx.DELETED{unknown}]{unknown} = 0) or (vibrato_preset[preset_idx.DELETED{unknown}]{unknown} = 1)) and (btn_scanPresets{unknown} -> key_alt = TRUE{unknown}))
				message("Scanning for deleted"){Builtin, None}
				if(not array_equal(vibrato_preset{unknown}, vibrato_preset2{unknown}){Builtin, None})
					vibPresetNames[presetCount{unknown}]{unknown} := fs_get_filename(get_ui_id(file_browser{unknown}){Builtin, None}, 0){Builtin, None}
					vibPresetCount[presetCount{unknown}]{unknown} := 1
					inc(presetCount{unknown}){Builtin, None}
					vibrato_preset[preset_idx.DELETED{unknown}]{unknown} := FALSE{unknown}
					save_array_str(vibrato_preset{unknown}, fs_get_filename(get_ui_id(file_browser{unknown}){Builtin, None}, 2){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
				end if
				array.clear(vibrato_preset{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
			end if
		end if
		btn_scanPresets{unknown} -> value := TRUE{unknown}
		fs_navigate(get_ui_id(file_browser{unknown}){Builtin, None}, 1){Builtin, None}
	else
		message("The end"){Builtin, None}
		save.resource_arrays{UserDefined, None}
		get.presetCount{UserDefined, None}
		preset_scan{unknown} := FALSE{unknown}
		btn_scanPresets{unknown} -> value := FALSE{unknown}
		update.preset.menu{UserDefined, None}
		load.preset{UserDefined, None}
	end if
end on

on ui_control(mnu_preset{unknown})
	call update.preset.menu{UserDefined, None}
	load.preset{UserDefined, None}
end on

on async_complete
	if(NI_ASYNC_ID{unknown} = save_id{unknown})
		if(NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS{unknown} = TRUE{unknown})
			save_id{unknown} := - 1
		else
			if(NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS{unknown} = FALSE{unknown})
				save_id{unknown} := 0
			end if
		end if
	end if
	if(NI_ASYNC_ID{unknown} = load_id{unknown})
		if(NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS{unknown} = TRUE{unknown})
			load_id{unknown} := - 1
		else
			if(NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS{unknown} = FALSE{unknown})
				load_id{unknown} := 0
			end if
		end if
	end if
end on

end on

end function

function get_num_groups_legato(num_dynamic_layers0 : unknown, rrs0 : unknown, mics0 : unknown, trans_groups0 : unknown, sustain_fx0 : unknown)
	return (((((((((((title_groups{unknown} + rrs0{unknown}) + title_groups{unknown}) + num_dynamic_layers0{unknown}) + title_groups{unknown}) + num_dynamic_layers0{unknown}) + title_groups{unknown}) + (num_dynamic_layers0{unknown} * sustain_fx0{unknown})) + title_groups{unknown}) + trans_groups0{unknown}) + title_groups{unknown}) + num_dynamic_layers0{unknown})
end function

function get_num_groups_one_shot(num_dynamic_layers1 : unknown, rrs1 : unknown, mics1 : unknown)
	return (title_groups{unknown} + rrs1{unknown})
end function

function get_num_groups_sustain(num_dynamic_layers2 : unknown, rrs2 : unknown, mics2 : unknown)
	return (((title_groups{unknown} + num_dynamic_layers2{unknown}) + title_groups{unknown}) + num_dynamic_layers2{unknown})
end function

function import_keyswitchArray
	for i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[keyswitch{unknown}, 1] - 1
		for j{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[keyswitch{unknown}, 2] - 1
			if(UI_keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown} # 0)
				select(j{unknown})
				case keyswitch_idx.NOTE{unknown}
					UI_keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown} -> value := search[keyswitches{unknown}, keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown}]
				case keyswitch_idx.NAME{unknown}
					UI_keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown} -> text := keyswitch_names[i{unknown}]{unknown}
				case keyswitch_idx.START_GROUP{unknown}
					UI_keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown} -> value := keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown} - title_groups{unknown}
				case keyswitch_idx.COLOR{unknown}
					UI_keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown} -> value := search[key_colors{unknown}, keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown}]
				case keyswitch_idx.ACTIVATE{unknown} to keyswitch_idx.COLOR{unknown}
					UI_keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown} -> value := keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown}
				case keyswitch_idx.PREFIX{unknown}
					UI_keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown} -> value := keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown}
				case keyswitch_idx.TRANSITION{unknown}
					UI_keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown} -> value := keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown}
				end select
			end if
		end for
	end for
end function

function export_keyswitchArray
	for i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[keyswitch{unknown}, 1] - 1
		for j{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[keyswitch{unknown}, 2] - 1
			select(j{unknown})
			case keyswitch_idx.NOTE{unknown}
				keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown} := keyswitches[UI_keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown} -> value]{unknown}
			case keyswitch_idx.NAME{unknown}
				keyswitch_names[i{unknown}]{unknown} := UI_keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown} -> text
			case keyswitch_idx.START_GROUP{unknown}
				keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown} := UI_keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown} -> value + title_groups{unknown}
			case keyswitch_idx.COLOR{unknown}
				keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown} := key_colors[UI_keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown} -> value]{unknown}
			case keyswitch_idx.ACTIVATE{unknown} to keyswitch_idx.COLOR{unknown}
				keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown} := UI_keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown} -> value
			case keyswitch_idx.PREFIX{unknown}
				keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown} := UI_keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown} -> value
			case keyswitch_idx.TRANSITION{unknown}
				keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown} := UI_keyswitch[i{unknown}, j{unknown}]{unknown} -> value
			end select
		end for
	end for
end function

function update.row_fonts
	for j{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[keyswitch{unknown}, 1] - 1
		for i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[keyswitch{unknown}, 2] - 1
			if(UI_keyswitch[j{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown} # 0)
				UI_keyswitch[j{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown} -> font_type := font.2pt8[UI_keyswitch[j{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.ACTIVATE{unknown}]{unknown} -> value, 0]{unknown}
			end if
		end for
	end for
end function

function analyze(keyswitch_idx0 : unknown)
	if(keyswitch[keyswitch_idx0{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.ACTIVATE{unknown}]{unknown} = TRUE{unknown})
		call reset.keycolors{UserDefined, None}
		get_keyrange(keyswitch_idx0{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
		fill_mapped_notes(keyswitch_idx0{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
		update.keycolor_mapped(keyswitch_idx0{unknown}, keyswitch[keyswitch_idx0{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.COLOR{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
		call analyze_vibrato_groups{UserDefined, None}
		call update.keyswitch{UserDefined, None}
	end if
end function

function analyze_vibrato_groups
	array.reset(vibrato_groups{unknown}, - 1){UserDefined, None}
	ii{unknown} := 0
	for i{unknown} := 0 to 16 - 1
		select(keyswitch[i{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.INSTRUMENT{unknown}]{unknown})
		case instrument.SUSTAIN{unknown}
			for j{unknown} := 0 to keyswitch[i{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER{unknown}]{unknown} - 1
				vibrato_groups[ii{unknown}]{unknown} := keyswitch[i{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.START_GROUP{unknown}]{unknown} + j{unknown}
				inc(ii{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			end for
		case instrument.LEGATO{unknown}
			for j{unknown} := 0 to ((keyswitch[i{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER{unknown}]{unknown} + title_groups{unknown}) + keyswitch[i{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER{unknown}]{unknown}) - 1
				vibrato_groups[ii{unknown}]{unknown} := ((keyswitch[i{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.START_GROUP{unknown}]{unknown} + keyswitch[i{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.RR_COUNT{unknown}]{unknown}) + title_groups{unknown}) + j{unknown}
				inc(ii{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			end for
		end select
	end for
end function

function keyswitchSettings.show(Boolean1 : unknown)
	btn_keyswitchSettings{unknown} := Boolean1{unknown}
	UI_keyswitchSettings{unknown} -> hide := hide_state[Boolean1{unknown}]{unknown}
end function

function fill_mapped_notes(keyswitch_idx1 : unknown)
	for keys{unknown} := 0 to 127
		keyswitch_mapped_notes[keyswitch_idx1{unknown}, keys{unknown}]{unknown} := FALSE{unknown}
		blip_note{unknown} := play_note(keys{unknown}, 1, 0, 1){Builtin, None}
		set_event_par_arr(blip_note{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		change_vol(blip_note{unknown}, - 2000000, 0){Builtin, None}
		set_event_par_arr(blip_note{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 1, keyswitch[keyswitch_idx1{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.START_GROUP{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		wait(1){Builtin, None}
		zone_id{unknown} := get_event_par(blip_note{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		if(zone_id{unknown} # - 1)
			message(zone_id{unknown} & ", " & keyswitch[keyswitch_idx1{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.START_GROUP{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			keyswitch_mapped_notes[keyswitch_idx1{unknown}, keys{unknown}]{unknown} := TRUE{unknown}
		end if
		fade_out(blip_note{unknown}, 0, 1){Builtin, None}
	end for
end function

function get_keyrange(keyswitch_idx2 : unknown)
	for keys{unknown} := 0 to 127
		blip_note{unknown} := play_note(keys{unknown}, 1, 0, 1){Builtin, None}
		set_event_par_arr(blip_note{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		change_vol(blip_note{unknown}, - 2000000, 0){Builtin, None}
		set_event_par_arr(blip_note{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 1, keyswitch[keyswitch_idx2{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.START_GROUP{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		wait(1){Builtin, None}
		zone_id{unknown} := get_event_par(blip_note{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		if(zone_id{unknown} # - 1)
			keyswitch[keyswitch_idx2{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.RANGE_LOW{unknown}]{unknown} := keys{unknown}
			message("Low: " & midi.note_names[keys{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			keys{unknown} := 127
		end if
		fade_out(blip_note{unknown}, 0, 1){Builtin, None}
	end for
	for keys{unknown} := 0 to 127
		blip_note{unknown} := play_note(127 - keys{unknown}, 1, 0, 1){Builtin, None}
		set_event_par_arr(blip_note{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		change_vol(blip_note{unknown}, - 2000000, 0){Builtin, None}
		set_event_par_arr(blip_note{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 1, keyswitch[keyswitch_idx2{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.START_GROUP{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		wait(1){Builtin, None}
		zone_id{unknown} := get_event_par(blip_note{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		if(zone_id{unknown} # - 1)
			keyswitch[keyswitch_idx2{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.RANGE_HIGH{unknown}]{unknown} := 127 - keys{unknown}
			message("High: " & midi.note_names[127 - keys{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			keys{unknown} := 127
		end if
		fade_out(blip_note{unknown}, 0, 1){Builtin, None}
	end for
end function

function color_keyswitches
	for key[0]{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[keyswitch{unknown}, 1] - 1
		set_key_color(keyswitches[key[0]{unknown}]{unknown}, KEY_COLOR_INACTIVE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		if((keyswitch[key[0]{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.ACTIVATE{unknown}]{unknown} = TRUE{unknown}) and (keyswitch[key[0]{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.NOTE{unknown}]{unknown} # 127))
			set_key_color(keyswitch[key[0]{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.NOTE{unknown}]{unknown}, KEY_COLOR_RED{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end for
end function

function update.keycolor_mapped(keyswitch_idx3 : unknown, color0 : unknown)
	for key[1]{unknown} := keyswitch[keyswitch_idx3{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.RANGE_LOW{unknown}]{unknown} to keyswitch[keyswitch_idx3{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.RANGE_HIGH{unknown}]{unknown}
		set_key_color(key[1]{unknown}, KEY_COLOR_INACTIVE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		if(keyswitch_mapped_notes[keyswitch_idx3{unknown}, key[1]{unknown}]{unknown} = TRUE{unknown})
			set_key_color(key[1]{unknown}, color0{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end for
end function

function reset.keycolors
	for key[1]{unknown} := 0 to 127
		set_key_color(key[1]{unknown}, KEY_COLOR_INACTIVE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	end for
end function

function purge.keyswitch(keyswitch_idx4 : unknown, state0 : unknown)
	start_group{unknown} := keyswitch[keyswitch_idx4{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.START_GROUP{unknown}]{unknown}
	num_dynamic_layers{unknown} := keyswitch[keyswitch_idx4{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER{unknown}]{unknown}
	rr_count{unknown} := keyswitch[keyswitch_idx4{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.RR_COUNT{unknown}]{unknown}
	mic_positions{unknown} := keyswitch[keyswitch_idx4{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.MIC_POSITIONS{unknown}]{unknown}
	num_transitions{unknown} := keyswitch[keyswitch_idx4{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.NUM_TRANSITIONS{unknown}]{unknown}
	sustain_fx{unknown} := keyswitch[keyswitch_idx4{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.SUSTAIN_FX{unknown}]{unknown}
	select(keyswitch[keyswitch_idx4{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.INSTRUMENT{unknown}]{unknown})
	case instrument.ONE_SHOT{unknown} to instrument.ADHSR{unknown}
		for key[4]{unknown} := start_group{unknown} to (start_group{unknown} + get_num_groups_one_shot(num_dynamic_layers{unknown}, rr_count{unknown}, mic_positions{unknown}){UserDefined, None}) - 1
			purge_group(key[4]{unknown}, state0{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		end for
	case instrument.SUSTAIN{unknown}
		for key[4]{unknown} := start_group{unknown} to (start_group{unknown} + get_num_groups_sustain(num_dynamic_layers{unknown}, rr_count{unknown}, mic_positions{unknown}){UserDefined, None}) - 1
			purge_group(key[4]{unknown}, state0{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		end for
	case instrument.LEGATO{unknown}
		for key[4]{unknown} := start_group{unknown} to (start_group{unknown} + get_num_groups_legato(num_dynamic_layers{unknown}, rr_count{unknown}, mic_positions{unknown}, num_transitions{unknown}, sustain_fx{unknown}){UserDefined, None}) - 1
			purge_group(key[4]{unknown}, state0{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		end for
	end select
end function

function update.keyswitch
	call reset.keycolors{UserDefined, None}
	for key[2]{unknown} := 0 to 16 - 1
		set_key_pressed(keyswitch[key[2]{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.NOTE{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitches_pressed[key[2]{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		btn_keyswitches[key[2]{unknown}]{unknown} -> value := keyswitches_pressed[key[2]{unknown}]{unknown}
		if(keyswitches_pressed[key[2]{unknown}]{unknown} = TRUE{unknown})
			update.keycolor_mapped(key[2]{unknown}, keyswitch[key[2]{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.COLOR{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
		end if
		if(keyswitch[key[2]{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.NOTE{unknown}]{unknown} = 127)
			keyswitches_pressed[key[2]{unknown}]{unknown} := TRUE{unknown}
		end if
		if(keyswitch[key[2]{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.ACTIVATE{unknown}]{unknown} = FALSE{unknown})
			keyswitches_pressed[key[2]{unknown}]{unknown} := FALSE{unknown}
		end if
	end for
	call color_keyswitches{UserDefined, None}
	for key[3]{unknown} := 0 to 16 - 1
		select(keyswitch[key[3]{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.INSTRUMENT{unknown}]{unknown})
		case instrument.SUSTAIN{unknown}
			for key[4]{unknown} := keyswitch[key[3]{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.RANGE_LOW{unknown}]{unknown} to keyswitch[key[3]{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.RANGE_HIGH{unknown}]{unknown}
				sustain_release(key[4]{unknown}, keyswitch_event_notes[key[3]{unknown}, key[4]{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch_event_ids[key[3]{unknown}, key[4]{unknown}]{unknown}, release_id{unknown}, keyswitch[key[3]{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.START_GROUP{unknown}]{unknown} + title_groups{unknown}, keyswitch[key[3]{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER{unknown}]{unknown}, keyswitch[key[3]{unknown}, keyswitch_idx.RR_COUNT{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
			end for
		case instrument.LEGATO{unknown}
			note_held{unknown} := 0

	return ((sh_right(val0{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None} .and. (1 * sh_left(1, 31 - pos0{unknown}){Builtin, None})) .or. sh_right(val0{unknown} .and. 2147483647, pos0{unknown}){Builtin, None})

function swap(a1 : unknown, b1 : unknown)
	a1{unknown} := a1{unknown} .xor. b1{unknown}
	b1{unknown} := b1{unknown} .xor. a1{unknown}
	a1{unknown} := a1{unknown} .xor. b1{unknown}
end function

function bitlist.reverse(bit_list11 : unknown)

function bitlist.swap(bit_list12 : unknown, idx10 : unknown, idx20 : unknown)

	declare local val_idx2 : unknown := bitlist.get(bit_list12{unknown}, idx20{unknown}){UserDefined, None} {Reuses: 0}

	bitlist.set(bit_list12{unknown}, idx20{unknown}, val_idx1{unknown}){UserDefined, None}

function vector.push_back(ls0 : unknown, val4 : unknown)
	ls0[max(1, ls0[0]{unknown} + 1){UserDefined, None}]{unknown} := val4{unknown}
	inc(ls0[0]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
end function

function vector.clear(ls1 : unknown)
	ls1[0]{unknown} := 0
end function

function vector.set(ls3 : unknown, idx4 : unknown, val5 : unknown)
	ls3[min(ls3[0]{unknown} + 1, idx4{unknown} + 1){UserDefined, None}]{unknown} := val5{unknown}
	if(idx4{unknown} > ls3[0]{unknown})
		inc(ls3[0]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	end if
end function

function vector.insert(ls4 : unknown, idx5 : unknown, val6 : unknown)
	if(idx5{unknown} > ls4[0]{unknown})
		vector.push_back(ls4{unknown}, val6{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	else
		for lib.i{unknown} := ls4[0]{unknown} downto idx5{unknown} + 1
			ls4[lib.i{unknown} + 1]{unknown} := ls4[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown}
		end for
		ls4[idx5{unknown} + 1]{unknown} := val6{unknown}
		inc(ls4[0]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	end if
end function

function vector.combine(ls5 : unknown, ls20 : unknown)
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to ls20[0]{unknown} - 1
		vector.push_back(ls5{unknown}, ls20[min(ls20[0]{unknown} + 1, lib.i{unknown} + 1){UserDefined, None}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	end for
end function

function vector.erase(ls6 : unknown, idx6 : unknown)
	if(idx6{unknown} < ls6[0]{unknown})
		for lib.i{unknown} := idx6{unknown} + 2 to ls6[0]{unknown}
			ls6[lib.i{unknown} - 1]{unknown} := ls6[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown}
		end for
	end if
	dec(ls6[0]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
end function

function vector.pop_back(ls7 : unknown) -> result : unknown
	result{unknown} := ls7[ls7[0]{unknown}]{unknown}
	dec(ls7[0]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
end function

function vector.print(ls8 : unknown)
	declare local l : string := "[" {Reuses: 0}

		l{unknown} := l{unknown} & ls8[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown}
		if(lib.i{unknown} < ls8[0]{unknown})
			l{unknown} := l{unknown} & ", "
		end if
	end for
	l{unknown} := l{unknown} & "]"
	message(l{unknown}){Builtin, None}
end function

function floatmask.sh_left(float_mask12 : unknown, pos1 : unknown)

		float_mask12[0]{unknown} := sh_left(float_mask12[0]{unknown}, pos1{unknown}){Builtin, None} .or. sh_right_safe(float_mask12[1]{unknown}, 32 - pos1{unknown}){UserDefined, None}

	else
		float_mask12[0]{unknown} := sh_left(float_mask12[1]{unknown}, pos1{unknown} - 32){Builtin, None}
		float_mask12[1]{unknown} := 0
	end if
end function

function floatmask.sh_right(float_mask13 : unknown, pos2 : unknown)

		float_mask13[1]{unknown} := sh_right_safe(float_mask13[1]{unknown}, pos2{unknown}){UserDefined, None} .or. sh_left(float_mask13[0]{unknown}, 32 - pos2{unknown}){Builtin, None}

	else

		float_mask13[0]{unknown} := 0
	end if
end function

function assert(func2 : unknown, expected0 : unknown)
	declare local result : unknown {Reuses: 0}
	if((tests.counter_successful{unknown} + tests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}) = 0)
		_test_init_message(tests.separator{string}){UserDefined, None}
		tests.time_init{unknown} := KSP_TIMER{unknown}
	end if
	tests.time_elapsed{unknown} := KSP_TIMER{unknown}
	result{unknown} := func2{unknown}
	tests.time_elapsed{unknown} := KSP_TIMER{unknown} - tests.time_elapsed{unknown}
	tests.time_end{unknown} := KSP_TIMER{unknown}
	if(result{unknown} = expected0{unknown})
		inc(tests.counter_successful{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		_test_message_successful(tests.counter_successful{unknown} + tests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}, result{unknown}, expected0{unknown}, tests.time_elapsed{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	else
		inc(tests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		_test_message_unsuccessful(tests.counter_successful{unknown} + tests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}, result{unknown}, expected0{unknown}, tests.time_elapsed{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	end if
end function

function assert_summary
	declare local success_rate : real {Reuses: 0}
	success_rate{unknown} := (int_to_real(tests.counter_successful{unknown}){Builtin, None} / int_to_real(tests.counter_successful{unknown} + tests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}){Builtin, None}) * 100
	_tests_summary_message(tests.separator{string}, tests.counter_successful{unknown} + tests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}, tests.time_init{unknown}, tests.time_end{unknown}, success_rate{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
end function

function assert_side_effects(func3 : unknown, variable0 : unknown, expected1 : unknown)
	if((stests.counter_successful{unknown} + stests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}) = 0)
		_test_init_message(stests.separator{string}){UserDefined, None}
		stests.time_init{unknown} := KSP_TIMER{unknown}
	end if
	stests.time_elapsed{unknown} := KSP_TIMER{unknown}
	func{Undefined, None}
	stests.time_elapsed{unknown} := KSP_TIMER{unknown} - stests.time_elapsed{unknown}
	stests.time_end{unknown} := KSP_TIMER{unknown}
	if(variable0{unknown} = expected1{unknown})
		inc(stests.counter_successful{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		_test_message_successful(stests.counter_successful{unknown} + stests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}, variable0{unknown}, expected1{unknown}, stests.time_elapsed{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	else
		inc(stests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		_test_message_unsuccessful(stests.counter_successful{unknown} + stests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}, variable0{unknown}, expected1{unknown}, stests.time_elapsed{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	end if
end function

function assert_side_effects_summary
	declare local success_rate : real {Reuses: 0}
	success_rate{unknown} := (int_to_real(stests.counter_successful{unknown}){Builtin, None} / int_to_real(stests.counter_successful{unknown} + stests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}){Builtin, None}) * 100
	_tests_summary_message(stests.separator{string}, stests.counter_successful{unknown} + stests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}, stests.time_init{unknown}, stests.time_end{unknown}, success_rate{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
end function

function _test_init_message(separator0 : unknown)
	message("RUN TESTS"){Builtin, None}
end function

function _test_message_successful(count0 : unknown, got0 : unknown, expected2 : unknown, time_elapsed0 : unknown)
	message("Test " & count0{unknown} & " SUCCEEDED Ran for " & time_elapsed0{unknown} & " ms."){Builtin, None}
end function

function _test_message_unsuccessful(count1 : unknown, got1 : unknown, expected3 : unknown, time_elapsed1 : unknown)
	message("Test " & count1{unknown} & " FAILED. Got " & got1{unknown} & ", expected " & expected3{unknown} & "." & " Ran for " & time_elapsed1{unknown} & " ms."){Builtin, None}
end function

function _tests_summary_message(separator1 : unknown, count2 : unknown, time_start0 : unknown, time_end0 : unknown, success_rate0 : unknown)
	message(separator1{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	message("TESTS SUMMARY"){Builtin, None}
	message("Ran " & count2{unknown} & " tests in " & (time_end0{unknown} - time_start0{unknown}) & " ms."){Builtin, None}
	message(success_rate0{unknown} & "% Success, " & tests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown} & " out of " & (tests.counter_successful{unknown} + tests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}) & " tests failed."){Builtin, None}
end function

function scale.range(input0 : unknown, currentMin0 : unknown, currentMax0 : unknown, scaleToMin0 : unknown, scaleToMax0 : unknown)
	return ((((input0{unknown} - currentMin0{unknown}) * (scaleToMax0{unknown} - scaleToMin0{unknown})) / (currentMax0{unknown} - currentMin0{unknown})) + scaleToMin0{unknown})
end function

function scale.range.real(input1 : unknown, currentMin1 : unknown, currentMax1 : unknown, scaleToMin1 : unknown, scaleToMax1 : unknown)
	return (real_to_int((((int_to_real(input1{unknown}){Builtin, None} - currentMin1{unknown}) * (scaleToMax1{unknown} - scaleToMin1{unknown})) / (currentMax1{unknown} - currentMin1{unknown})) + scaleToMin1{unknown}){Builtin, None})
end function

function scale.range.slider(input2 : unknown, scaleToMin2 : unknown, scaleToMax2 : unknown)
	return (real_to_int(((input2{unknown} * (scaleToMax2{unknown} - scaleToMin2{unknown})) / 1e+06) + scaleToMin2{unknown}){Builtin, None})
end function

function scale.slider(input3 : unknown, scaleToMin3 : unknown, scaleToMax3 : unknown)
	return (real_to_int(((int_to_real(input3{unknown}){Builtin, None} * (scaleToMax3{unknown} - scaleToMin3{unknown})) / 1e+06) + scaleToMin3{unknown}){Builtin, None})
end function

function scale.range.log(input4 : unknown, currentMin2 : unknown, currentMax2 : unknown, scaleToMin4 : unknown, scaleToMax4 : unknown)
	return (pow(10, (log(scaleToMin4{unknown}){Builtin, None} / log(10){Builtin, None}) + (((input4{unknown} - currentMin2{unknown}) / (currentMax2{unknown} - currentMin2{unknown})) * ((log(scaleToMax4{unknown}){Builtin, None} / log(10){Builtin, None}) - (log(scaleToMin4{unknown}){Builtin, None} / log(10){Builtin, None})))){Builtin, None})
end function

function scale.clamp.to(input5 : unknown, fromMin0 : unknown, fromMax0 : unknown, toMin0 : unknown, toMax0 : unknown)
	return (real_to_int(scale.range(int_to_real(((input5{unknown} * (1 + (sh_right(fromMax0{unknown} - input5{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None} .or. sh_right(input5{unknown} - fromMin0{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None}))) - (fromMin0{unknown} * sh_right(input5{unknown} - fromMin0{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None})) - (fromMax0{unknown} * sh_right(fromMax0{unknown} - input5{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None})){Builtin, None}, int_to_real(fromMin0{unknown}){Builtin, None}, int_to_real(fromMax0{unknown}){Builtin, None}, int_to_real(toMin0{unknown}){Builtin, None}, int_to_real(toMax0{unknown}){Builtin, None}){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None})
end function

function isBitSet(x7 : unknown, pos3 : unknown)
	return (sh_right(x7{unknown}, pos3{unknown}){Builtin, None} .and. 1)
end function

function set_bit(x8 : unknown, pos4 : unknown)
	return (x8{unknown} .or. sh_left(1, pos4{unknown}){Builtin, None})
end function

function clear_bit(x9 : unknown, pos5 : unknown)
	return (x9{unknown} .and. .not. sh_left(1, pos5{unknown}){Builtin, None})
end function

function flip_bit(x10 : unknown, pos6 : unknown)
	return (.not. (.not. (x10{unknown} .and. .not. (x10{unknown} .and. sh_left(1, pos6{unknown}){Builtin, None})) .and. .not. (sh_left(1, pos6{unknown}){Builtin, None} .and. .not. (x10{unknown} .and. sh_left(1, pos6{unknown}){Builtin, None}))))
end function

function modify_bit(x11 : unknown, pos7 : unknown, state1 : unknown)
	return (.not. (.not. ((x11{unknown} .and. .not. sh_left(1, pos7{unknown}){Builtin, None}) .and. .not. ((x11{unknown} .and. .not. sh_left(1, pos7{unknown}){Builtin, None}) .and. (- state1{unknown} .and. sh_left(1, pos7{unknown}){Builtin, None}))) .and. .not. ((- state1{unknown} .and. sh_left(1, pos7{unknown}){Builtin, None}) .and. .not. ((x11{unknown} .and. .not. sh_left(1, pos7{unknown}){Builtin, None}) .and. (- state1{unknown} .and. sh_left(1, pos7{unknown}){Builtin, None})))))
end function

function decimal.to.binary(input6 : unknown, output_array0 : unknown)
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[output_array0{unknown}] - 2
		output_array0[(num_elements[output_array0{unknown}] - 2) - lib.i{unknown}]{unknown} := abs(sh_right(- (input6{unknown} .and. sh_left(1, lib.i{unknown}){Builtin, None}), 31){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	end for
end function

function binary.to.decimal(length0 : unknown, input_array0 : unknown) -> result : unknown
	result{unknown} := 0
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to length0{unknown} - 1
		result{unknown} := result{unknown} + (input_array0[(length0{unknown} - 1) - lib.i{unknown}]{unknown} * real_to_int(pow(2, int_to_real(lib.i{unknown}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None})
	end for
end function

function clamp(x12 : unknown, min0 : unknown, max0 : unknown)
	return (((x12{unknown} * is_in_range(x12{unknown}, min0{unknown}, max0{unknown}){UserDefined, None}) - (min0{unknown} * sh_right(x12{unknown} - min0{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None})) - (max0{unknown} * sh_right(max0{unknown} - x12{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None}))
end function

function clamp.slider(x13 : unknown)
	return ((x13{unknown} * is_in_range(x13{unknown}, 0, 1000000){UserDefined, None}) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - x13{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None}))
end function

function clip(x14 : unknown, top0 : unknown)
	return ((x14{unknown} * is_in_range(x14{unknown}, 0, top0{unknown}){UserDefined, None}) - (top0{unknown} * sh_right(top0{unknown} - x14{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None}))
end function

function max(a7 : unknown, b7 : unknown)
	return (a7{unknown} - ((a7{unknown} - b7{unknown}) .and. sh_right(a7{unknown} - b7{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None}))
end function

function max4(a8 : unknown, b8 : unknown, c0 : unknown, d0 : unknown)
	return (max(a8{unknown}, b8{unknown}){UserDefined, None} - ((max(a8{unknown}, b8{unknown}){UserDefined, None} - max(c0{unknown}, d0{unknown}){UserDefined, None}) .and. sh_right(max(a8{unknown}, b8{unknown}){UserDefined, None} - max(c0{unknown}, d0{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, 31){Builtin, None}))
end function

function min(a9 : unknown, b9 : unknown)
	return (a9{unknown} - ((a9{unknown} - b9{unknown}) .and. sh_right(b9{unknown} - a9{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None}))
end function

function min4(a10 : unknown, b10 : unknown, c1 : unknown, d1 : unknown)
	return (min(a10{unknown}, b10{unknown}){UserDefined, None} - ((min(a10{unknown}, b10{unknown}){UserDefined, None} - min(c1{unknown}, d1{unknown}){UserDefined, None}) .and. sh_right(min(c1{unknown}, d1{unknown}){UserDefined, None} - min(a10{unknown}, b10{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, 31){Builtin, None}))
end function

function div(x15 : unknown, y2 : unknown)
	return ((x15{unknown} + (x15{unknown} mod y2{unknown})) / y2{unknown})
end function

function log(base0 : unknown, value2 : unknown)
	return (log(value2{unknown}){Builtin, None} / log(int_to_real(base0{unknown}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None})
end function

function decimals(value3 : unknown, div0 : unknown, dec_div0 : unknown)
	return ((value3{unknown} / div0{unknown}) & '.' & abs((value3{unknown} mod div0{unknown}) / dec_div0{unknown}){Builtin, None})
end function

function fmod(a11 : unknown, b11 : unknown)
	return (a11{unknown} - (floor(a11{unknown} / b11{unknown}){Builtin, None} * b11{unknown}))
end function

function trim(input7 : unknown, decim0 : unknown)
	return (round(input7{unknown} * pow(10, int_to_real(decim0{unknown}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None} / pow(10, int_to_real(decim0{unknown}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None})
end function

function non_rpt_random(last_random0 : unknown, min_random0 : unknown, max_random0 : unknown) -> result : unknown
	result{unknown} := Rand(min_random0{unknown} + 1, max_random0{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	result{unknown} := (last_random0{unknown} + result{unknown}) mod (max_random0{unknown} + 1)
	last_random0{unknown} := result{unknown}
end function

function Rand(min1 : unknown, max1 : unknown) -> result : unknown
	___M.Seed{unknown} := (8088405 * ___M.Seed{unknown}) + 1
	result{unknown} := ((sh_right(___M.Seed{unknown}, 8){Builtin, None} .and. 16777215) mod ((max1{unknown} - min1{unknown}) + 1)) + min1{unknown}
end function

function RandomSeed
	___M.Seed{unknown} := KSP_TIMER{unknown}
end function

function ResetRand
	___M.Seed{unknown} := 1107155288
end function

function save.preset
	load_id{unknown} := load_array_str(vibrato_preset{unknown}, vibrato_path{string} & txt_presetName{string} & ".nka"){Builtin, None}
	wait_async(load_array_str(vibrato_preset{unknown}, vibrato_path{string} & txt_presetName{string} & ".nka"){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	if(load_id{unknown} # - 1)
		vibPresetCount[presetCount{unknown}]{unknown} := 1
		vibPresetNames[presetCount{unknown}]{string} := txt_presetName{string}
		save.resource_arrays{UserDefined, None}
		mnu_preset{unknown} := presetCount{unknown}
		presetCount{unknown} := clamp(presetCount{unknown} + 1, 0, 100){UserDefined, None}
		preset_scan{unknown} := TRUE{unknown}
		btn_scanPresets{unknown} -> picture := "alpha"
	end if
	vibrato_preset[preset_idx.DELETED{unknown}]{unknown} := FALSE{unknown}
	for i{unknown} := preset_idx.BODY{unknown} to 100 - 1
		if(uiControls[i{unknown} - preset_idx.BODY{unknown}]{unknown} # 0)
			vibrato_preset[i{unknown}]{unknown} := uiControls[i{unknown} - preset_idx.BODY{unknown}]{unknown} -> value
		end if
	end for
	save_array_str(vibrato_preset{unknown}, vibrato_path{string} & txt_presetName{string} & ".nka"){Builtin, None}
	call update.preset.menu{UserDefined, None}
end function

function delete.preset
	vibrato_preset[preset_idx.DELETED{unknown}]{unknown} := TRUE{unknown}
	save_array_str(vibrato_preset{unknown}, vibrato_path{string} & vibPresetNames[mnu_preset{unknown}]{string} & ".nka"){Builtin, None}
	ii{unknown} := 0
	for i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[vibPresetCount{unknown}] - 1
		if(i{unknown} # mnu_preset{unknown})
			vibPresetNames[ii{unknown}]{unknown} := vibPresetNames[i{unknown}]{unknown}
			vibPresetCount[ii{unknown}]{unknown} := vibPresetCount[i{unknown}]{unknown}
			inc(ii{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end for
	save.resource_arrays{UserDefined, None}
	presetCount{unknown} := clamp(presetCount{unknown} - 1, 0, 100){UserDefined, None}
	mnu_preset{unknown} := clamp(mnu_preset{unknown} - 1, 0, presetCount{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	call update.preset.menu{UserDefined, None}
	if(presetCount{unknown} # 0)
		load.preset{UserDefined, None}
	end if
end function

function load.preset
	wait_async(load_array_str(vibrato_preset{unknown}, vibrato_path{string} & vibPresetNames[mnu_preset{unknown}]{string} & ".nka"){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	message("load preset: " & ", " & vibrato_path{string} & vibPresetNames[mnu_preset{unknown}]{string} & ".nka"){Builtin, None}
	call load.array{UserDefined, None}
end function

function load.array
	for i{unknown} := preset_idx.BODY{unknown} to 100 - 1
		if(uiControls[i{unknown} - preset_idx.BODY{unknown}]{unknown} # 0)
			uiControls[i{unknown} - preset_idx.BODY{unknown}]{unknown} -> value := vibrato_preset[i{unknown}]{unknown}
		end if
	end for
	for i{unknown} := 0 to search[vibrato_groups{unknown}, - 1] - 1
		set_engine_par(ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[0]{unknown}, sli_envRateCurve{unknown}, vibrato_groups[i{unknown}]{unknown}, find_mod(vibrato_groups[i{unknown}]{unknown}, "ENV_AHDSR"){Builtin, None}, - 1){Builtin, None}
	end for
	tbl_rate.curve{unknown} := sli_envRateCurve{unknown}

function update.preset.menu
	if(presetCount{unknown} = 0)
		txt_presetName{unknown} -> text := "EMPTY PRESET"
	else
		txt_presetName{unknown} -> text := vibPresetNames[mnu_preset{unknown} -> value]{string}
	end if
	for i{unknown} := 0 to 100 - 1
		if(i{unknown} < presetCount{unknown})
			set_menu_item_str(get_ui_id(mnu_preset{unknown}){Builtin, None}, i{unknown}, vibPresetNames[i{unknown}]{string}){Builtin, None}
			set_menu_item_visibility(get_ui_id(mnu_preset{unknown}){Builtin, None}, i{unknown}, TRUE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		else
			set_menu_item_visibility(get_ui_id(mnu_preset{unknown}){Builtin, None}, i{unknown}, FALSE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end for
end function

function home.show(Boolean3 : unknown)
	btn_home{unknown} := Boolean3{unknown}
	UI_home{unknown} -> hide := hide_state[Boolean3{unknown}]{unknown}
	UI_reverb{unknown} -> hide := hide_state[Boolean3{unknown}]{unknown}
	UI_eq{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
end function

function settings.show(Boolean4 : unknown)
	btn_settings{unknown} := Boolean4{unknown}
	UI_settings{unknown} -> hide := hide_state[Boolean4{unknown}]{unknown}
end function

function sustain(event_note0 : unknown, event_notes0 : unknown, event_velocity0 : unknown, note_id0 : unknown, start_group0 : unknown, num_dynamic_layers3 : unknown, num_rr0 : unknown)
	if(event_notes0{unknown} = - 1)
		event_notes0{unknown} := event_note0{unknown}
		note_id0{unknown} := play_note(event_note0{unknown}, event_velocity0{unknown}, 0, 0){Builtin, None}
		set_event_par_arr(note_id0{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		for dyn{unknown} := 0 to num_dynamic_layers3{unknown} - 1
			set_event_par_arr(note_id0{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 1, dyn{unknown} + start_group0{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		end for
	end if
end function

function sustain_release(release_note0 : unknown, event_notes1 : unknown, note_id1 : unknown, release_id0 : unknown, start_group1 : unknown, num_dynamic_layers4 : unknown, num_rr1 : unknown)
	if(note_id1{unknown} # - 1)
		note_off(note_id1{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		release_id0{unknown} := play_note(release_note0{unknown}, 50, 0, 0){Builtin, None}
		set_event_par_arr(release_id0{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		for dyn_release{unknown} := 0 to num_dynamic_layers4{unknown} - 1
			set_event_par_arr(release_id0{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 1, ((dyn_release{unknown} + start_group1{unknown}) + num_dynamic_layers4{unknown}) + title_groups{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		end for
		note_id1{unknown} := - 1
		event_notes1{unknown} := - 1
	end if
end function

function one_shot(event_note1 : unknown, event_notes2 : unknown, event_velocity1 : unknown, note_id2 : unknown, start_group2 : unknown, num_rr2 : unknown, rr_counter0 : unknown, sample_duration0 : unknown)
	if(event_notes2{unknown} # event_note1{unknown})
		event_notes2{unknown} := event_note1{unknown}
		rr_counter0{unknown} := (rr_counter0{unknown} + 1) mod num_rr2{unknown}
		note_id2{unknown} := play_note(event_note1{unknown}, event_velocity1{unknown}, 0, sample_duration0{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		set_event_par_arr(note_id2{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		set_event_par_arr(note_id2{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 1, rr_counter0{unknown} + start_group2{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	end if
end function

function one_shot_release(release_note1 : unknown, event_notes3 : unknown, note_id3 : unknown)
	note_id3{unknown} := - 1
	event_notes3{unknown} := - 1
end function

function legato.load_arrays(prefix_idx0 : unknown)
	wait_async(load_array_str(trans_file_names{unknown}, legato_path{string} & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx0{unknown}]{string} & "trans_file_names.nka"){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	wait_async(load_array_str(intervals{unknown}, legato_path{string} & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx0{unknown}]{string} & "intervals.nka"){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	wait_async(load_array_str(trans_zone_ids{unknown}, legato_path{string} & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx0{unknown}]{string} & "trans_zone_ids.nka"){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	wait_async(load_array_str(trans_zone_start{unknown}, legato_path{string} & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx0{unknown}]{string} & "trans_zone_start.nka"){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	wait_async(load_array_str(trans_event_volume{unknown}, legato_path{string} & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx0{unknown}]{string} & "trans_event_volume.nka"){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	wait_async(load_array_str(trans_wait_time{unknown}, legato_path{string} & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx0{unknown}]{string} & "trans_wait_time.nka"){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	wait_async(load_array_str(trans_fadeIn_time{unknown}, legato_path{string} & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx0{unknown}]{string} & "trans_fadeIn_time.nka"){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	wait_async(load_array_str(trans_fadeOut_time{unknown}, legato_path{string} & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx0{unknown}]{string} & "trans_fadeOut_time.nka"){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	wait_async(load_array_str(sus_release_time{unknown}, legato_path{string} & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx0{unknown}]{string} & "sus_release_time.nka"){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	wait_async(load_array_str(sus_fadeIn_time{unknown}, legato_path{string} & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx0{unknown}]{string} & "sus_fadeIn_time.nka"){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	wait_async(load_array_str(marked_samples{unknown}, legato_path{string} & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx0{unknown}]{string} & "marked_samples.nka"){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	wait_async(load_array_str(sample_comments{unknown}, legato_path{string} & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx0{unknown}]{string} & "sample_comments.nka"){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	wait_async(load_array_str(file_names_master{unknown}, legato_path{string} & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx0{unknown}]{string} & "file_names_master.nka"){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	wait_async(load_array_str(zone_ids_master{unknown}, legato_path{string} & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx0{unknown}]{string} & "zone_ids_master.nka"){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	wait_async(load_array_str(completed_elements{unknown}, legato_path{string} & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx0{unknown}]{string} & "completed_elements.nka"){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	legato.init_arrays{UserDefined, None}
end function

function legato.init_arrays
	for i{unknown} := 0 to 2000 - 1
		if(sus_release_time[i{unknown}]{unknown} = 0)
			sus_release_time[i{unknown}]{unknown} := DEFAULT_VAL.sus_release_time{unknown}
		end if
		if(trans_fadeIn_time[i{unknown}]{unknown} = 0)
			trans_fadeIn_time[i{unknown}]{unknown} := DEFAULT_VAL.trans_fadeIn_time{unknown}
		end if
		if(trans_fadeOut_time[i{unknown}]{unknown} = 0)
			trans_fadeOut_time[i{unknown}]{unknown} := DEFAULT_VAL.trans_fadeOut_time{unknown}
		end if
		if(trans_wait_time[i{unknown}]{unknown} = 0)
			trans_wait_time[i{unknown}]{unknown} := DEFAULT_VAL.trans_wait_time{unknown}
		end if
		if(sus_fadeIn_time[i{unknown}]{unknown} = 0)
			sus_fadeIn_time[i{unknown}]{unknown} := DEFAULT_VAL.sus_fadeIn_time{unknown}
		end if
		if(trans_zone_ids[i{unknown}]{unknown} = 0)
			trans_zone_ids[i{unknown}]{unknown} := - 1
		end if
	end for
end function

function get_bit_id(event_id0 : unknown)
	return ((sh_left(lsb(abs(trans_group{unknown} - get_zone_par(get_event_par(event_id0{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID{unknown}){Builtin, None}, ZONE_PAR_GROUP{unknown}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}, 14){Builtin, None} .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par(event_id0{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID{unknown}){Builtin, None}, ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO{unknown}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}, 7){Builtin, None}) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par(event_id0{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID{unknown}){Builtin, None}, ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY{unknown}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None})
end function

function get_trans_idx(event_id1 : unknown) -> result : unknown
	if(search[trans_zone_ids{unknown}, get_bit_id(event_id1{unknown}){UserDefined, None}] = - 1)
		result{unknown} := search[trans_zone_ids{unknown}, - 1]
	else
		result{unknown} := search[trans_zone_ids{unknown}, get_bit_id(event_id1{unknown}){UserDefined, None}]
	end if
end function

function legato(note1 : unknown, event_notes4 : unknown, note_id4 : unknown, old_note_id0 : unknown, start_group3 : unknown, num_dynamic_layers5 : unknown, num_rr3 : unknown, trans_groups1 : unknown, sustain_fx1 : unknown, current_trans_group0 : unknown, rr_counter1 : unknown)
	atk_group{unknown} := start_group3{unknown}
	atk_sus_group{unknown} := (atk_group{unknown} + num_rr3{unknown}) + title_groups{unknown}
	sus_group{unknown} := (atk_sus_group{unknown} + num_dynamic_layers5{unknown}) + title_groups{unknown}
	sus_fx_group{unknown} := (sus_group{unknown} + num_dynamic_layers5{unknown}) + title_groups{unknown}
	trans_group{unknown} := (sus_fx_group{unknown} + (num_dynamic_layers5{unknown} * sustain_fx1{unknown})) + title_groups{unknown}
	sus_rls_group{unknown} := (trans_group{unknown} + trans_groups1{unknown}) + title_groups{unknown}
	num_notes{unknown} := 0
	message(keyswitches[16 - 1]{unknown} + 1){Builtin, None}
	for i{unknown} := keyswitches[16 - 1]{unknown} + 1 to num_elements[KEY_DOWN{unknown}] - 1
		num_notes{unknown} := KEY_DOWN[i{unknown}]{unknown} + num_notes{unknown}
	end for
	message("num_notes: " & num_notes{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	interval{unknown} := EVENT_NOTE{unknown} - last_note{unknown}
	if(((num_notes{unknown} > 1) and (note1{unknown} # last_note{unknown})) and (is_attack{unknown} # - 1))
		is_attack{unknown} := FALSE{unknown}
		if(abs(interval{unknown}){Builtin, None} <= 12)
			blip_note{unknown} := play_note((note1{unknown} * ne(ge(interval{unknown}, 0){UserDefined, None}){UserDefined, None}) + (last_note{unknown} * ge(interval{unknown}, 0){UserDefined, None}), (abs(interval{unknown}){Builtin, None} * 5) + (ge(interval{unknown}, 0){UserDefined, None} * 60), 0, - 1){Builtin, None}
			change_vol(blip_note{unknown}, - 200000, 0){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(blip_note{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(blip_note{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 1, trans_group{unknown} + current_trans_group0{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			wait(1){Builtin, None}
			trans_idx{unknown} := get_trans_idx(blip_note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
			fade_out(old_note_id0{unknown}, sus_release_time[trans_idx{unknown}]{unknown} * 1000, 1){Builtin, None}
			old_note_id0{unknown} := - 1
			fade_out(last_transition{unknown}, 240000, 1){Builtin, None}
			fade_out(blip_note{unknown}, 1, 1){Builtin, None}
			transition_id{unknown} := play_note((note1{unknown} * ne(ge(interval{unknown}, 0){UserDefined, None}){UserDefined, None}) + (last_note{unknown} * ge(interval{unknown}, 0){UserDefined, None}), (abs(interval{unknown}){Builtin, None} * 5) + (ge(interval{unknown}, 0){UserDefined, None} * 60), real_to_int((int_to_real(trans_zone_start[trans_idx{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 48000) * 1e+06){Builtin, None}, 0){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(transition_id{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(transition_id{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{unknown}, trans_fadeIn_time[trans_idx{unknown}]{unknown}, 3){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(transition_id{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{unknown}, trans_fadeOut_time[trans_idx{unknown}]{unknown}, 5){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(transition_id{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 1, trans_group{unknown} + current_trans_group0{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			change_vol(transition_id{unknown}, trans_event_volume[trans_idx{unknown}]{unknown}, 0){Builtin, None}
			note_id4{unknown} := play_note(note1{unknown}, 69, sus_s_start{unknown}, - 1){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(note_id4{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{unknown}, trans_wait_time[trans_idx{unknown}]{unknown}, 0){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(note_id4{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{unknown}, sus_fadeIn_time[trans_idx{unknown}]{unknown}, 2){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(note_id4{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			for i{unknown} := 0 to num_dynamic_layers5{unknown} - 1
				set_event_par_arr(note_id4{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 1, i{unknown} + sus_group{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			end for
			for i{unknown} := 0 to (num_dynamic_layers5{unknown} * sustain_fx1{unknown}) - 1
				set_event_par_arr(note_id4{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 1, i{unknown} + sus_fx_group{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			end for
		else
			fade_out(old_note_id0{unknown}, 152 * 1000, 1){Builtin, None}
			old_note_id0{unknown} := - 1
			note_id4{unknown} := play_note(note1{unknown}, EVENT_VELOCITY{unknown}, sus_s_start{unknown}, - 1){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(note_id4{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{unknown}, 150000, 0){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(note_id4{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{unknown}, DEFAULT_VAL.sus_fadeIn_time{unknown}, 2){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(note_id4{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			for i{unknown} := 0 to num_dynamic_layers5{unknown} - 1
				set_event_par_arr(note_id4{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 1, i{unknown} + sus_group{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			end for
			for i{unknown} := 0 to (num_dynamic_layers5{unknown} * sustain_fx1{unknown}) - 1
				set_event_par_arr(note_id4{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 1, i{unknown} + sus_fx_group{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			end for
		end if
	else
		if(num_notes{unknown} = 1)
			message("Initial Note"){Builtin, None}
			last_note{unknown} := note1{unknown}
			is_attack{unknown} := - 1
			set_event_par_arr(ALL_EVENTS{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			is_attack{unknown} := ne(NOTE_HELD{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
			note_id4{unknown} := play_note(note1{unknown}, 69, 250000, - 1){Builtin, None}
			attack_id{unknown} := play_note(note1{unknown}, min(clamp(EVENT_VELOCITY{unknown}, CC[103]{unknown} - 20, CC[103]{unknown} + 20){UserDefined, None}, 127){UserDefined, None}, 0, 0){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(note_id4{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			for key[5]{unknown} := 0 to num_dynamic_layers5{unknown} - 1
				set_event_par_arr(note_id4{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 1, key[5]{unknown} + atk_sus_group{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			end for
			for key[5]{unknown} := 0 to (num_dynamic_layers5{unknown} * sustain_fx1{unknown}) - 1
				set_event_par_arr(note_id4{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 1, key[5]{unknown} + sus_fx_group{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			end for
			set_event_par_arr(attack_id{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 1, atk_group{unknown} + rr_counter1{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			rr_counter1{unknown} := (rr_counter1{unknown} + 1) mod num_rr3{unknown}
		else
			note_off(note_id4{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end if
	last_transition{unknown} := transition_id{unknown}
	last_note{unknown} := note1{unknown}
	event_notes4{unknown} := note1{unknown}
end function

function legato_release(release_note2 : unknown, event_notes5 : unknown, note_id5 : unknown, release_id1 : unknown, start_group4 : unknown, num_dynamic_layers6 : unknown, num_rr4 : unknown, trans_groups2 : unknown)
	if((note_held{unknown} = 0) and (note_id5{unknown} # - 1))
		event_notes5{unknown} := - 1
		note_id5{unknown} := - 1
		count{unknown} := 0
		if(is_attack{unknown} = FALSE{unknown})
			release_id1{unknown} := play_note(get_event_par(note_id5{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_NOTE{unknown}){Builtin, None}, 50, 0, 0){Builtin, None}
			set_event_par_arr(release_id1{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 0, ALL_GROUPS{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			for key[6]{unknown} := 0 to num_dynamic_layers6{unknown} - 1
				set_event_par_arr(release_id1{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, 1, ((((((((((key[6]{unknown} + start_group4{unknown}) + num_rr4{unknown}) + title_groups{unknown}) + num_dynamic_layers6{unknown}) + title_groups{unknown}) + num_dynamic_layers6{unknown}) + title_groups{unknown}) + (num_dynamic_layers6{unknown} * sustain_fx{unknown})) + title_groups{unknown}) + trans_groups2{unknown}) + title_groups{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			end for
		end if
		playpos{unknown} := clamp(get_event_par(note_id5{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_PLAY_POS{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 10, 0, 140000){UserDefined, None}
		fade_out(note_id5{unknown}, real_to_int(scale.range(int_to_real(playpos{unknown}){Builtin, None}, 0, 140000, 1, 230000){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None}, 1){Builtin, None}
		change_vol(release_id1{unknown}, - real_to_int(scale.range(int_to_real(playpos{unknown}){Builtin, None}, 0, 140000, 10000, 500){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None}, 0){Builtin, None}
		get_event_ids(active_ids{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		for key[6]{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[active_ids{unknown}] - 1
			if(not ((note_id5{unknown} = active_ids[key[6]{unknown}]{unknown}) or (release_id1{unknown} = active_ids[key[6]{unknown}]{unknown})))
				fade_out(active_ids[key[6]{unknown}]{unknown}, 250000, 1){Builtin, None}
			end if
		end for
	end if
end function

	development[0]{unknown} := - 1

	if(_id{unknown} = - 1)
	end if
end function

	disable_logging(NI_LOG_MESSAGE{unknown}){Builtin, None}

	disable_logging(NI_LOG_WATCHING{unknown}){Builtin, None}
end function

	if(_id{unknown} = - 1)
	end if
end function

function find_nka(array9 : unknown, nka0 : unknown, search_depth0 : unknown) -> result : unknown
	declare local parent : string {Reuses: 0}
	declare local it : unknown {Reuses: 0}
	it{unknown} := 0
	parent{string} := ""
	_id{unknown} := load_array_str(array9{unknown}, get_folder(GET_FOLDER_PATCH_DIR{unknown}){Builtin, None} & parent{unknown} & nka0{unknown} & ".nka"){Builtin, None}
	while((_id{unknown} # - 1) and (it{unknown} < search_depth0{unknown})) 
		parent{unknown} := parent{unknown} & "../"
		_id{unknown} := load_array_str(array9{unknown}, get_folder(GET_FOLDER_PATCH_DIR{unknown}){Builtin, None} & parent{unknown} & nka0{unknown} & ".nka"){Builtin, None}
		inc(it{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	end while
	result{unknown} := get_folder(GET_FOLDER_PATCH_DIR{unknown}){Builtin, None} & parent{unknown} & nka0{unknown} & ".nka"
end function

function find_key_nka(array10 : unknown, nka1 : unknown, key0 : unknown, parent_folder0 : unknown, search_depth1 : unknown) -> result : unknown
	declare local path : string {Reuses: 0}
	declare local it : unknown {Reuses: 0}
	array10[0]{unknown} := - 1
	it{unknown} := 0
	path{string} := ""
	_id{unknown} := load_array_str(array10{unknown}, get_folder(GET_FOLDER_PATCH_DIR{unknown}){Builtin, None} & path{unknown} & parent_folder0{unknown} & nka1{unknown} & ".nka"){Builtin, None}
	while(((_id{unknown} # - 1) and (it{unknown} < search_depth1{unknown})) and (array10[0]{unknown} # key0{unknown})) 
		array10[0]{unknown} := - 1
		path{unknown} := path{unknown} & "../"
		_id{unknown} := load_array_str(array10{unknown}, get_folder(GET_FOLDER_PATCH_DIR{unknown}){Builtin, None} & path{unknown} & parent_folder0{unknown} & nka1{unknown} & ".nka"){Builtin, None}
		inc(it{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	end while
	result{unknown} := get_folder(GET_FOLDER_PATCH_DIR{unknown}){Builtin, None} & path{unknown} & nka1{unknown} & ".nka"
end function
